They also didn't seem built to hold a decent amount of hair on the curler, it was just kind of a mess. Pros - quick heat, if you leave them on long enough they get good and hot, easy to use, and an on/off switch Cons - curlers can get super hot, clips can get super hot, clips leave unsightly creases, and don't hold hair on the curler all that well.
